        <script type="javascript/blocked">
        (function() {
            // Wrap in IIFE to avoid global scope pollution
            function initYouTubeButtons() {
                // Function to create and insert YouTube buttons
                function createYouTubeButtons(container) {
                    const subscribeUrl = container.dataset.subscribeUrl;
                    const watchUrl = container.dataset.watchUrl;
                    
                    const buttonsHtml = `
                        <a href="${subscribeUrl}" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="aegis-youtube-subscribe-button">
                            📺 Subscribe To Us On YouTube
                        </a>
                        <a href="${watchUrl}" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="aegis-youtube-watch-button">
                            ▶️ Watch On YouTube
                        </a>
                    `;
                    
                    container.innerHTML = buttonsHtml;
                    container.classList.add("loaded");
                }
                
                // Intersection Observer for lazy loading
                if (window.IntersectionObserver) {
                    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
                        entries.forEach(function(entry) {
                            if (entry.isIntersecting && !entry.target.classList.contains("loaded")) {
                                createYouTubeButtons(entry.target);
                                observer.unobserve(entry.target);
                            }
                        });
                    }, {
                        rootMargin: "50px 0px",
                        threshold: 0.1
                    });
                    
                    // Observe all lazy YouTube button containers
                    const lazyContainers = document.querySelectorAll(".aegis-lazy-youtube-buttons");
                    lazyContainers.forEach(function(container) {
                        observer.observe(container);
                    });
                } else {
                    // Fallback for browsers that don't support IntersectionObserver
                    const lazyContainers = document.querySelectorAll(".aegis-lazy-youtube-buttons");
                    lazyContainers.forEach(function(container) {
                        createYouTubeButtons(container);
                    });
                }
            }
            
            // Use multiple event listeners to ensure compatibility
            if (document.readyState === "loading") {
                document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", initYouTubeButtons);
            } else {
                // DOM is already loaded
                initYouTubeButtons();
            }
        })();
        </script>

<h1>Content No Longer Available</h1>
<p id="fpo0">The article or other content you were looking for was part of our archived content from our previous news feed system and is no longer available on our site. The webpage’s link may have also been changed or updated.</p>
